    2624                 :            : 
    2625                 :            : /**
    2626                 :            :  * Return a height-based locktime for new transactions (uses the height of the
    2627                 :            :  * current chain tip unless we are not synced with the current chain
    2628                 :            :  */
    2629                 :        663 : static uint32_t GetLocktimeForNewTransaction(interfaces::Chain& chain, interfaces::Chain::Lock& locked_chain)
    2630                 :            : {
    2631                 :        663 :     uint32_t const height = locked_chain.getHeight().get_value_or(-1);
    2632                 :            :     uint32_t locktime;
    2633                 :            :     // Discourage fee sniping.
    2634                 :            :     //
    2635                 :            :     // For a large miner the value of the transactions in the best block and
    2636                 :            :     // the mempool can exceed the cost of deliberately attempting to mine two
    2637                 :            :     // blocks to orphan the current best block. By setting nLockTime such that
    2638                 :            :     // only the next block can include the transaction, we discourage this
    2639                 :            :     // practice as the height restricted and limited blocksize gives miners
    2640                 :            :     // considering fee sniping fewer options for pulling off this attack.
    2641                 :            :     //
    2642                 :            :     // A simple way to think about this is from the wallet's point of view we
    2643                 :            :     // always want the blockchain to move forward. By setting nLockTime this
    2644                 :            :     // way we're basically making the statement that we only want this
    2645                 :            :     // transaction to appear in the next block; we don't want to potentially
    2646                 :            :     // encourage reorgs by allowing transactions to appear at lower heights
    2647                 :            :     // than the next block in forks of the best chain.
    2648                 :            :     //
    2649                 :            :     // Of course, the subsidy is high enough, and transaction volume low
    2650                 :            :     // enough, that fee sniping isn't a problem yet, but by implementing a fix
    2651                 :            :     // now we ensure code won't be written that makes assumptions about
    2652                 :            :     // nLockTime that preclude a fix later.
    2653         [ +  + ]:        663 :     if (IsCurrentForAntiFeeSniping(chain, locked_chain)) {
    2654                 :        662 :         locktime = height;
    2655                 :            : 
    2656                 :            :         // Secondly occasionally randomly pick a nLockTime even further back, so
    2657                 :            :         // that transactions that are delayed after signing for whatever reason,

    3811                 :            : /**
    3812                 :            :  * Compute smart timestamp for a transaction being added to the wallet.
    3813                 :            :  *
    3814                 :            :  * Logic:
    3815                 :            :  * - If sending a transaction, assign its timestamp to the current time.
    3816                 :            :  * - If receiving a transaction outside a block, assign its timestamp to the
    3817                 :            :  *   current time.
    3818                 :            :  * - If receiving a block with a future timestamp, assign all its (not already
    3819                 :            :  *   known) transactions' timestamps to the current time.
    3820                 :            :  * - If receiving a block with a past timestamp, before the most recent known
    3821                 :            :  *   transaction (that we care about), assign all its (not already known)
    3822                 :            :  *   transactions' timestamps to the same timestamp as that most-recent-known
    3823                 :            :  *   transaction.
    3824                 :            :  * - If receiving a block with a past timestamp, but after the most recent known
    3825                 :            :  *   transaction, assign all its (not already known) transactions' timestamps to
    3826                 :            :  *   the block time.
    3827                 :            :  *
    3828                 :            :  * For more information see CWalletTx::nTimeSmart,
    3829                 :            :  * https://bitcointalk.org/?topic=54527, or
    3830                 :            :  * https://github.com/bitcoin/bitcoin/pull/1393.
    3831                 :            :  */
